  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_5b506985-2aa3-4836-8287-7e6c017b906a'
      });
    }

  <span id="freeText2244097943230318655" style="display:none">New York Times <i>bestselling author Lynsay Sands delivers a wickedly fun Argeneau novel featuring a vampire ready to claim his mate and the beauty who resists her fate!</i><br /><br /><b>A kiss doesn’t mean eternity . . .</b><br /><br />Valerie Moyer doesn’t believe in vampires—until she is kidnapped by a fanged psychopath! After escaping her bloodthirsty captor, she’s through with creatures of the night. Until she finds herself under the protection of the darkly handsome Anders. Not only is she expected to accept that Anders is immortal, but also that she is the woman destined to be his life mate!<br /><br /><b>. . . Or does it?</b><br /><br />Anders felt a connection to Valerie from the moment he cradled her bruised body in his arms. But before he claims her, he must destroy the vampire who almost stole her from him forever. His job would be easier if Valerie didn’t fight him every step of the way. Still, Anders loves a challenge, and the green-eyed beauty is worth fighting for!</span>

<div id="review_542843041" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/542843041" />
    <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish"><img alt="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1398981306p2/1113032.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/542843041?book_show_action=true">Feb 21, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="user" itemprop="url" name="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish">UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=author-lynsay-sands">author-lynsay-sands</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=pnr-vampires">pnr-vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=publisher-avon-books">publisher-avon-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=own-have-read">own-have-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=series-argeneau">series-argeneau</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=avon-addict-reads">avon-addict-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=4-stars">4-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=2013-reads">2013-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=pnr-vampire-enforcers">pnr-vampire-enforcers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer542843041" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1323551175880454577"><br/><b>
  <i>Immortal Ever After</i>
</b> is the 18th book in Lynsay Sands’ insanely popular <i>Argeneau</i> series, and a fun, exciting, sexy story! I’ve read more than my fair share of the paranormal romance genre, most especially vampires. I don’t know what it is, but there’s something about these tormented souls that draw me in and keep me coming back for more. It’s not often that I fall in love during my first read of a series, but I fell - and fell hard - for the <i>Argeneau</i> world. <blockquote><i>From the cover:</i><br/><br/><b>A kiss doesn’t mean </b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText1323551175880454577" style="display:none"><br /><b>
  <i>Immortal Ever After</i>
</b> is the 18th book in Lynsay Sands’ insanely popular <i>Argeneau</i> series, and a fun, exciting, sexy story! I’ve read more than my fair share of the paranormal romance genre, most especially vampires. I don’t know what it is, but there’s something about these tormented souls that draw me in and keep me coming back for more. It’s not often that I fall in love during my first read of a series, but I fell - and fell hard - for the <i>Argeneau</i> world. <blockquote><i>From the cover:</i><br /><br /><b>A kiss doesn’t mean eternity . . .</b><br /><br />Valerie Moyer doesn’t believe in vampires—until she is kidnapped by a fanged psychopath! After escaping her bloodthirsty captor, she’s through with creatures of the night. Until she finds herself under the protection of the darkly handsome Anders. Not only is she expected to accept that Anders is immortal, but also that she is the woman destined to be his life mate!<br /><br /><b>. . . Or does it?</b><br /><br />Anders felt a connection to Valerie from the moment he cradled her bruised body in his arms. But before he claims her, he must destroy the vampire who almost stole her from him forever. His job would be easier if Valerie didn’t fight him every step of the way. Still, Anders loves a challenge, and the green-eyed beauty is worth fighting for!</blockquote> <i>Immortal Ever After</i> is my first taste of Lynsay Sands’ writing and I was very pleased! This world she’s created is exciting, and the characters are intriguing, compelling, and very sexy.<br /><br />I usually <i>hate</i> coming into a series mid-way because I either end up lost or cringing at the information dump we have to endure. Thankfully, I was neither lost nor cringing because Ms. Sands did a great job of giving us the <i>Argeneau</i> world background without making me feel like I was reading a text book. The story is well written and through dialog between characters – old and new – she imparts everything new readers need to know to feel like we’re part of the story, not just reading about it.<br /><br />Anders is such a great guy! I can see why everyone loves him, and anyone who’s been anxiously awaiting his story will be very happy! He’s so much fun… open but shy, strong but vulnerable, and not just sexy but super sexy! He’s the kind of vampire I want for my very own!<br /><br />Valerie is a great heroine. What she’s endured would break most women, but not her. Even though everything she ever thought she knew about the world around her has been turned upside down, she holds it together and does what she has to to survive. <br /><br />The bottom line: In case you didn’t get it, I really enjoyed this book, and while it was my first experience with Ms. Sands’ <i>Argeneau</i> series, it most certainly will not be my last!<br /><br /><i>My thanks to Avon Books for providing me with a copy of this story I exchange for an honest review.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="1323551175880454577" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2054660446" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2054660446" />
    <a title="Jilly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly"><img alt="Jilly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435955932p2/25894509.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2054660446?book_show_action=true">Jul 10, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jilly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jilly" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly">Jilly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2054660446" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7000546678895811524">Can I be let-down when I end up liking a book that I was expecting to hate? You know that book rants are like chocolate to me. I need. I crave. I indulge way too much to be considered normal.<br/><br/>The hero of this book is called Anders and he was kind of a dick in past books. I was looking forward to him acting like an alpha-asshole and me getting to call him an alpha-asshole. It's my thing. I even have a bookshelf dedicated to them. I feel really good when I rail on an A.A., and I get my feminist car</span>
  <span id="freeText7000546678895811524" style="display:none">Can I be let-down when I end up liking a book that I was expecting to hate? You know that book rants are like chocolate to me. I need. I crave. I indulge way too much to be considered normal.<br><br>The hero of this book is called Anders and he was kind of a dick in past books. I was looking forward to him acting like an alpha-asshole and me getting to call him an alpha-asshole. It's my thing. I even have a bookshelf dedicated to them. I feel really good when I rail on an A.A., and I get my feminist card punched. Just two more to go and I get a free sandwich - made by a man of course.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1499745126i/23263020.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, imagine my surprise when Anders turned into a sweet, fuzzy teddy bear when he meets his life-mate. What the hell, Anders? He was a gushy pile of goo. I actually kind of liked him. A total sweetie.<br><br>I liked his love-interest too. She was nice, smart enough, and even saved a house full of women who were being tortured. She never acted too-stupid-to-live. She wasn't a damsel in distress. And, yet she wasn't annoyingly perky or quirky or sassy. Damn! This means I liked both of the MC's.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1499745126i/23263023.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, how am I supposed to review this book? Don't worry, friends. There were still some things I could make fun of. Isn't there always?<br><br>First, let's start with the fact that our main girl, Valerie (see? not even a stupid name), is a veterinarian and has an awesome German Shepherd. You know that I love dogs and think cats are the spawn of satan. Well, Valerie is one of those dog owners who has the dog so well trained, they are like some sort of indoctrinated, kool-ade drinking minion who frankly creeps everyone out. You know the type - the dog isn't allowed on furniture, to eat scraps, has to go through a bunch of tricks to get their food dish filled, sits and waits for the owner's word before walking out a door, etc... Meanwhile, my dogs and I are laying on the couch eating pizza. My dogs didn't want me to continue reading when they saw this turn of events. It became a "scary movie" night after that. We needed our throw blanket and some stuffed animals to cuddle.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1499745126i/23263022.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Next, I need to mention the fact that although she doesn't have an idiotic name, and he is called "Anders", we find out his real first name in this book and I'm kind of mad. I mean, why would anyone do this to a character? His name is Semen. That's right. Semen. And, if that isn't bad enough, she starts calling him Semmy. She calls out "Semmy" in the throes of passion and we are supposed to just take this lying down? No. Just no.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1499745126i/23263021.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The dog is right. Ain't nobody got time for that kind of bullshit.<br><br>And, my final complaint? These vampire cops are dumb, man. I mean, come on. They should actually be smarter than mortal cops. They have been around for thousands of years. And yet, they always make stupid bone-head moves that make me shake my head. They also never seem to see the most obvious traps or bad guys that a teenager from a horror movie would spot. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1499745126i/23263019._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh well. At least they are pretty.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7000546678895811524" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/491144206?book_show_action=true">Dec 31, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer491144206" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7294552891811660946">Another great addition to the Argeneau series. Read this one in less than 24 hours, it just grabbed me from page one. It seems like the books in this series are either very light hearted and almost silly in the angst that the characters get into or they are darker and more serious and meaty while still being such fun to read. Immortal Ever After is definitely one of the more serious additions to this long running series. I love the way that this author weaves humor, strong alpha males and stubbo</span>
  <span id="freeText7294552891811660946" style="display:none">Another great addition to the Argeneau series. Read this one in less than 24 hours, it just grabbed me from page one. It seems like the books in this series are either very light hearted and almost silly in the angst that the characters get into or they are darker and more serious and meaty while still being such fun to read. Immortal Ever After is definitely one of the more serious additions to this long running series. I love the way that this author weaves humor, strong alpha males and stubborn independent females all around either an outrageously wild situation or a very serious threat. In this book we get to catch a glimpse of past leads and see how they are doing after their H.E.A, and with 18 titles there are plenty of characters I would love to see again, I must re-read this series sometime. We get to see one of my favorite former Alpha leads who is always so tough and scary but still lovable, Lucian and his life mate Leigh as they reach the end of Leigh's pregnancy. It was really fun to watch as they drove each other nuts with Leigh's independent streak and Lucian's overbearing protectiveness. I really do recommend this series to my friends that love paranormal, they are great books that will suck you in and leave you laughing out loud.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17001748242986911084"> <br/><br/><br/>Readers will fall in love with this romantic urban fantasy . Lynsay Sands gets back to what works best with the latest in her popular Argeneau Family series . Rogue Hunter , Anders , finds his life mate in Valerie...not your usual damsel in distress . <br/>Valerie is the perfect life mate for the uber- sexy Anders . This girl don't need no hero . Kidnapped & caged by a psycho vampire wanna be intent on making her his midnight snack, fiesty Valerie makes good her own escape . By staking one of her ki</span>
  <span id="freeText17001748242986911084" style="display:none"> <br /><br /><br />Readers will fall in love with this romantic urban fantasy . Lynsay Sands gets back to what works best with the latest in her popular Argeneau Family series . Rogue Hunter , Anders , finds his life mate in Valerie...not your usual damsel in distress . <br />Valerie is the perfect life mate for the uber- sexy Anders . This girl don't need no hero . Kidnapped &amp; caged by a psycho vampire wanna be intent on making her his midnight snack, fiesty Valerie makes good her own escape . By staking one of her kidnappers she saves not only her own chops but the rest of the menu as well . Her 911 call brings Anders &amp; his crew of hunters . <br />Anders unexpectantly finds his life mate when he answers a 911 call . He realizes that he can't read Valerie's mind . He has found his life mate at long last ...and she's just been ravaged by one of his own kind . Clearly , she's gonna need some time to ease into a trusting relationship before he reveals the truth to her . But how much time does he have when her captor - a rogue - starts hunting his victims . <br />I loved this story . Sands injected it with her trademark brand of suspence , humor , &amp; steamy sex . It's a sexy read loaded with plenty of action . We see lots of old faces . Lucian &amp; Leigh &amp; their bundle of joy get lots of face time . Immortal Ever After is a must read for fans of the Argeneau Family series . Fans old &amp; new are gonna love it ! I'm giving it a high five for Lynsay Sands &amp; her latest hit .<br /><br />ARC downloaded courtesy of Avon Publishing &amp; Edelweiss . <br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_408139603" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/408139603" />
    <a title="Terree" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5633810-terree"><img alt="Terree" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1337330161p2/5633810.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/408139603?book_show_action=true">Sep 05, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Terree" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Terree" href="/user/show/5633810-terree">Terree</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer408139603" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7732649696718001901">The anticipation of reading this book for me was almost overwhelming! For those of you who read the Argeneau series, you know the character Marguerite. Well… I am a Marguerite groupie! What is that? You ask? Well, this woman thinks it is her sole duty to see all of the people she comes in contact with in any slight way to be matched with their Life Mates, those who they will spend eternity with… blissfully! <br/><br/>This book was about Anders (one I love), an Enforcer for the Immortals, ensuring that the</span>
  <span id="freeText7732649696718001901" style="display:none">The anticipation of reading this book for me was almost overwhelming! For those of you who read the Argeneau series, you know the character Marguerite. Well… I am a Marguerite groupie! What is that? You ask? Well, this woman thinks it is her sole duty to see all of the people she comes in contact with in any slight way to be matched with their Life Mates, those who they will spend eternity with… blissfully! <br /><br />This book was about Anders (one I love), an Enforcer for the Immortals, ensuring that the laws aren’t broken and when they are… well, he and his fellow enforcers are there to take care of things, a police officer for Immortals if you will. I was just so happy. Part of the job as an enforcer is to monitor the mortal police radio to see if odd calls come through, things with key words, vampire, bite, stake and… well you get the idea. So when a call came through with those very words they checked it out to see if it was a Vampire Wannabe or something more sinister, known to the enforcers as Rogues.<br /><br />Valerie had spent 10 days drugged in a cage that she could barely sit up in with a freak who thought he was a vampire! He had captured quite a few women, kept them in the dark and barely fed and had his minion Igor as they had come to call him, drag one of them up basement stairs every night so his boss could practice gnawing on necks and drain them of blood in the process, at least that is what she assumed happened.<br /><br />For a full review follow this link:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.thewindowseat13.com/2013/02/lynsay-sands-immortal-ever-after.html">http://www.thewindowseat13.com/2013/0...</a><br /></span>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7607772777795306267">Solid 4 stars! It's an Argeneau novel after all. : )<br/><br/>IMMORTAL EVER AFTER, an Argeneau novel by Lynsay Sands is, as always expected from Lynsay, a delightful read, threaded with humor, danger, and of course, plenty of steamy seduction on the part of Anders, but I was surprised and excited about how singular and independent Valerie Moyer was in every situation. She's a heroine to admire. She's not afraid to take matters into her own hands whether it is escaping from a rogue immortal or seducing And</span>
  <span id="freeText7607772777795306267" style="display:none">Solid 4 stars! It's an Argeneau novel after all. : )<br /><br />IMMORTAL EVER AFTER, an Argeneau novel by Lynsay Sands is, as always expected from Lynsay, a delightful read, threaded with humor, danger, and of course, plenty of steamy seduction on the part of Anders, but I was surprised and excited about how singular and independent Valerie Moyer was in every situation. She's a heroine to admire. She's not afraid to take matters into her own hands whether it is escaping from a rogue immortal or seducing Anders because she just can't resist climbing such an incredibly tall drink of water. I wish it had been a tad bit longer and had a bit more action but it was still a wonderful read and I loved the inclusion of Roxy, a faithful and loyal canine companion. It was a joy to be witness to the domestication of Lucian, and of course, it's always a joy to have that adorable Justin Bricker hanging around as well as many of our other favorites.<br /> <br />I highly recommend IMMORTAL EVER AFTER by Lynsay Sands to anyone who has never read an Argeneau novel, because once you read this one, you'll definitely be scrambling to read more. For those Argeneau fans who have waited patiently for Anders HEA, it's here, and you're going to fall madly in love with this man. As if we weren't already halfway there with his strong, silent type aura that has always surrounded him. Lynsay has come through once again to provide us with an endearing, exciting, and as ever, romantic happy-ever-after paranormal romance.<br /><br />***eARC provided by publisher in exchange for an honest and unscripted review.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7607772777795306267" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15414635203867258394">I enjoyed this book as I have all the Argeneau books. It has the same quirky sense of humor and several characters from previous books make an appearance adding to the feeling of "a visit home". <br/><br/>In life I would probably like Valerie and Anders very much. They are loyal, intelligent, and have a good solid dose of common sense that is admirable. Valerie is a strong heroine, saving herself several times which is a nice change of pace.<br/><br/>My problem with the book was the two protagonists weren't all tha</span>
  <span id="freeText15414635203867258394" style="display:none">I enjoyed this book as I have all the Argeneau books. It has the same quirky sense of humor and several characters from previous books make an appearance adding to the feeling of "a visit home". <br /><br />In life I would probably like Valerie and Anders very much. They are loyal, intelligent, and have a good solid dose of common sense that is admirable. Valerie is a strong heroine, saving herself several times which is a nice change of pace.<br /><br />My problem with the book was the two protagonists weren't all that exciting. Their story was as laid back as their personalities, but it lacked oomph. I also felt as though I was being told how Valerie and Anders felt, not shown. An example of this is the nightmares Valerie had after her ordeal. We were told she had them, but that was about the extent of it - very little real emotion.<br /><br />Still, a solid read about a group of immortals (don't call them vampires, they don't like that term - lol) that I enjoy visiting, and characters I would love to meet.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15414635203867258394" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Darcy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2225246-darcy"><img alt="Darcy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1293937643p2/2225246.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/381064901?book_show_action=true">Jul 31, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Darcy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Darcy" href="/user/show/2225246-darcy">Darcy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780062078124" href="/book/show/17191641-immortal-ever-after">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2225246-darcy?shelf=e-book">e-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2225246-darcy?shelf=2013">2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2225246-darcy?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2225246-darcy?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer381064901" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10309427258527382062">Like many long running series, you go into them knowing what to expect, that is what this series is for me. They are filled with light, fluffy, fun.<br/><br/>I loved Valerie, loved that she didn't wait around for someone to save her, but went about saving herself. I really liked that Anders knew she was his life mate, which helped set up things for later. For some reason I found all the action in Leigh and Lucian's house to be funny, mostly because the action wasn't action per se, but the normal everyday </span>
  <span id="freeText10309427258527382062" style="display:none">Like many long running series, you go into them knowing what to expect, that is what this series is for me. They are filled with light, fluffy, fun.<br /><br />I loved Valerie, loved that she didn't wait around for someone to save her, but went about saving herself. I really liked that Anders knew she was his life mate, which helped set up things for later. For some reason I found all the action in Leigh and Lucian's house to be funny, mostly because the action wasn't action per se, but the normal everyday routine of the immortals trying to hide what they were. I think by allowing Valerie to get to know them in this normal way helped her accept things. <br /><br />It was funny how Valerie found out about the immortals. I loved how Anders kept making her promise to listen and not walk away. Almost as funny was when Valerie first saw Bricker feed. Her checking out his teeth like a horse had me laughing. <br /><br />Leigh kept me laughing all through this one with her pushy ways making everyone do what she wanted them to. I also loved her getting back at Lucian by programing certain ring tones to his phone. I did admire her when trouble seemed to find her and Valerie at the same time she went into labor.<br /><br />On a side note, I have to say that I loved Anders real name!! I can just see the author sitting down and coming up with the name, then having to stop writing to laugh her ass off. Then once her hands are steady and the tears cleaned up from her face, her letting her other author friends know, causing more peels of laughter.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10309427258527382062" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer464061021" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer12683103465517348250">You can find this review and more at <a href='http://foreverbklover.blogspot.com/2013/03/immortal-ever-after-argeneau-18-by.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Forever Book Lover.</a><br/><br/>I am a stalker when it comes to the Argeneau series, so when I saw this as an ARC in edelweiss I requested it without any idea of who the main characters were or what the plot was!! <br/><br/>This started out very very dark, honestly it was a bit scary. It did not start out as a Lynsay Sand's typical lighthearted Argeneau book. Someone was kidnapping women, drugging them and keeping them prisoner in a small cage. What was scary was that the guard wou</span>
  <span id="freeText12683103465517348250" style="display:none">You can find this review and more at <a href="http://foreverbklover.blogspot.com/2013/03/immortal-ever-after-argeneau-18-by.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Forever Book Lover.</a><br /><br />I am a stalker when it comes to the Argeneau series, so when I saw this as an ARC in edelweiss I requested it without any idea of who the main characters were or what the plot was!! <br /><br />This started out very very dark, honestly it was a bit scary. It did not start out as a Lynsay Sand's typical lighthearted Argeneau book. Someone was kidnapping women, drugging them and keeping them prisoner in a small cage. What was scary was that the guard would take one of the girls where they would become the "toy" for a sadistic vampire.. Luckily, the sexy Anders is nearby and is just the perfect bodyguard that Valerie needs.. In the previous books in this series, Anders is always portrayed as a loner, a quiet one... but it was fun reading how he deals with finding his life mate. Wait until you hear the "nickname" Valerie gives him, LOL. This book is filled with twists and turns until a final showdown at the end... <br /><br />We see our favorite vampire/lifemate couples throughout this story, like a homecoming. I love the antics of Leigh, she is hilarious. As this is the 18th book in the series, I am wondering if it will continue, I think all of the main and secondary characters have had their story told, well the only one i think left my be Justin. I hate to see this series end, but we may have run out of romance and life mates to pair up.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16826416188477905036">First of all, the cover. Is this man hugging some sort of architectural element? Not a winner.<br/><br/>I liked this book. It seemed to be a return somewhat to the earlier feel of the series. I have a tendency to like stories about the older vampires. The heroine was very nice. She was plucky and very resourceful and it seemed natural that she would respond well to the idea of vampires/immortals given how she was written. I thought Anders was well written and sweet. I liked the scenes from his POV where h</span>
  <span id="freeText16826416188477905036" style="display:none">First of all, the cover. Is this man hugging some sort of architectural element? Not a winner.<br /><br />I liked this book. It seemed to be a return somewhat to the earlier feel of the series. I have a tendency to like stories about the older vampires. The heroine was very nice. She was plucky and very resourceful and it seemed natural that she would respond well to the idea of vampires/immortals given how she was written. I thought Anders was well written and sweet. I liked the scenes from his POV where he was coming to terms with what he felt for her and how he planned to convince her to turn.<br /><br />It was lovely to see so much of Lucien and Leigh. I wasn't as fond of the books that wandered to far from the Argeneaus. This book wasn't part of an overarching plot line which is fine with me. It was more of a day in the life sort of book. I many times prefer that sort. The guys are out on a routine rogue call and one of them meets his life mate. It's all wrapped up in one book and the next one can be another guy on another day.<br /><br />Fans of the series should like this one and it wouldn't be hard to pick up the series here if you were a newby. It would be easy to understand what was going on.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16826416188477905036" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_486511488" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/486511488" />
    <a title="Carey Sabala" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6574584-carey-sabala"><img alt="Carey Sabala" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1371352955p2/6574584.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/486511488?book_show_action=true">Dec 27, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carey Sabala" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carey Sabala" href="/user/show/6574584-carey-sabala">Carey Sabala</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer486511488" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4878922066216837251">The book features our hero Anders and our heroine Valerie. It starts off with Valerie being kidnapped and held hostage with 6 other young women. Each are kept drugged and in cages and are brought out for dinner one night a week. The women can't see each other due to being kept in a dark basement but find talking to each other helps sooth some of the horror. All the women believe that the guy and his helper (dubbed Igor) are crazy, that he's living some weird Vampire fantasy. Eventually Valerie r</span>
  <span id="freeText4878922066216837251" style="display:none">The book features our hero Anders and our heroine Valerie. It starts off with Valerie being kidnapped and held hostage with 6 other young women. Each are kept drugged and in cages and are brought out for dinner one night a week. The women can't see each other due to being kept in a dark basement but find talking to each other helps sooth some of the horror. All the women believe that the guy and his helper (dubbed Igor) are crazy, that he's living some weird Vampire fantasy. Eventually Valerie realizes that their food is being drugged and decides that she will forego her daily meal of oatmeal and water to keep her wits about her when it's time for her night out. When her night arrives, she is lucid enough to concoct an escape plan. She pretends at first to be drugged, all the while looking for anything that can be used as a weapon. When she is dragged into an upstairs bathroom, she jumps her assailant and stakes him. She, of course, finds a phone to call 911 but then hears the garage door opening and realizes that who she assaulted was only Igor and the bigger threat is on his way to her. After she calls 911, she makes her escape through a window, knowing the police won't make it in time to help her. <br />Enter our hero, Anders. His group of Vampire/Immortal enforcers have waylaid the 911 call and have arrived at the house in question to clean up the rouge immortals' mess and bring him to justice without letting the mortals know their kind exist. After a thorough investigation and look around the property, Anders ends up finding Valerie passed out in the bushes due to her injuries, starvation and a jump from a two-story house. When Anders decides to try to give her some medical attention, she ends up waking up in the process and it's at that moment, when Anders tries to enter her mind to soothe her, that he realizes he can't read her......(queue the "dun, dun, dun" music). <br />OK enough spoilers! If you aren't familiar with Lynsay Sands Argeneau Series, It's about a family of Immortal Atlantians who were subject to an Atlantian medical experiment gone array. They were injected with Nanos but when Atlantis fell, no one was there to help take them out. The Nanos have evolved to give the descendants the classic "Vampire" attributes but they claim they are not vampires. Anywho, one of the attributes is a selection process by the Nanos for their host in which they choose the perfect "life mate" and one of the tale tell signs is not being able to mind read that person. <br />All the false Vampire/Atlantian stuff aside, Lynsay Sands has brought to the PNR world a wonderful series with the Argeneau's. It's definitely a classic HEA based in the PNR world. Each book features some descendant from the original Argeneau family or central character to the books. They are definitely fun reads with very strong characters. What I loved most about this book is that the heroine, Valerie, is definitely not the typical female PNR mortal character waiting for rescue from the big sexy Vampire man. All through the book, she is rescuing herself and/or others. Anders very rarely is on the scene when rescuing is needed, which is actually kind of funny.<br />As a fan of the series, I definitely thought this was a great addition to the ongoing series and would highly recommend it for a PNR read. </span>
  <a data-text-id="4878922066216837251" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1694196994" />

        <a title="Rachel Beamin&#39;" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel Beamin&#39;" href="/user/show/17627552-rachel-beamin">Rachel Beamin&#39;</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17627552-rachel-beamin?shelf=dnf">dnf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17627552-rachel-beamin?shelf=meh">meh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17627552-rachel-beamin?shelf=vampys">vampys</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1694196994" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17633915795281528251">Maybe I am in a book rut. Maybe I have read all the good ones, but everything I have touched in the last couple of days have been less than stellar. I started this series on book whatever, of course not starting with book 1. <br/>It would also appear that I am the only one out of 8,000 readers that found this less than 18 stars. GO ME. <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492198131ra/22493055.gif' width='350' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>If you are looking for a good book to put you to sleep, you have stumbled across the right one. Despite me liking Anders, Leigh, Lucian, even Margarite (to be honest, </span>
  <span id="freeText17633915795281528251" style="display:none">Maybe I am in a book rut. Maybe I have read all the good ones, but everything I have touched in the last couple of days have been less than stellar. I started this series on book whatever, of course not starting with book 1. <br>It would also appear that I am the only one out of 8,000 readers that found this less than 18 stars. GO ME. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492198131ra/22493055.gif" width="350" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>If you are looking for a good book to put you to sleep, you have stumbled across the right one. Despite me liking Anders, Leigh, Lucian, even Margarite (to be honest, I have no fucking clue where this character even popped up from), I couldn’t stomach Valerie. Every time she spoke I was tempted to bash my face into my kindle. <br>Here goes:<br>Valerie is kidnapped and stuffed into a small 4x4x4x4 cage. She is housed in the basement with 6 other women. Valerie was chosen, on this lucky day, to be taken to the “Master”, on her “outing” she stabs Igor in the heart with a table leg, freeing herself and the other women. <br>At this point, the enforcers show up. <i>Oooohhhh…..</i><br>Anders falls madly in love with Valerie and wants to bond with her. <i>Isn’t that sweet…</i><br>Valerie is one of those heroines who don’t know what she wants. <i>Do I want to shave my legs? Yes, but wait no I don’t. I will shave half of my leg, which will show the world I can make my own decisions.</i> One second she doesn’t want Anders near her and hides in her room, the next she is stripping and making the “O” face.<br>Anders is in a predicament, does he tell the insta-love-of-his-life about who he really is? Hell, he doesn’t even know who he is. Is he a vampire? According to him he is NOT. But yet, he has to drink blood to live and is immortal, oh and he can read minds and manipulate humans. <i>If you have to drink blood to survive, I would say you are Vampire.</i><br>Now, on to the whole “do I tell her or not?” At what point do you think it is a good idea to hold a secret from a female? We are Fort Knox with remembering betrayals, <b>
  <i>WE DO NOT FORGET</i>
</b>. To be honest if she is stripping and allowing you in the golden cave of love, I highly doubt she will care what you are. Just saying.<br>With all that being said, I got through 50% of this oh inspiring book, deleted it from my kindle and shut the blasted thing off. <br></span>

          </span>

<div id="review_551897507" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/551897507" />
    <a title="Paulina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4156141-paulina"><img alt="Paulina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1281896379p2/4156141.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/551897507?book_show_action=true">Mar 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Paulina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Paulina" href="/user/show/4156141-paulina">Paulina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer551897507" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18259699825478986574">I liked this book well enough. As with the others in this series, it's a light, fun read. However, sloppy writing and dumb decisions by a secondary female caused me to get pulled out of the story a few times while reading it. The sloppy writing I'm referring to mostly happened at the beginning of the book, where the heroine would say something about herself (ex, she took martial arts lessons) to the hero, and then the information would be repeated to the hero a few pages later, and he would act </span>
  <span id="freeText18259699825478986574" style="display:none">I liked this book well enough. As with the others in this series, it's a light, fun read. However, sloppy writing and dumb decisions by a secondary female caused me to get pulled out of the story a few times while reading it. The sloppy writing I'm referring to mostly happened at the beginning of the book, where the heroine would say something about herself (ex, she took martial arts lessons) to the hero, and then the information would be repeated to the hero a few pages later, and he would act as though he had never heard the information. So, either the book needed some more editing, or the hero is a little mentally deficient. Luckily, this only happened a few times, mainly while the background of the heroine was being revealed. The main thing I've grown tired of in this series are the dumb decisions that the females make. It's not that they're TSTL, it's just that they act in ways that seem to be uncharacteristic - it's as though the writer can't think of any other way to put them in danger. **SPOILERISH** For example, if Veronica is being stalked by two rogues, why would Leigh encourage her to leave the safe house just because Leigh didn't want to pee in someone eles's house? And why would Veronica agree to go? I mean, really?? **END SPOILER**<br /><br />Neither of these were enough to keep me from enjoying the book, but they did lower my rating of this book from almost 4 stars down to about 3.25. I am looking forward to reading the next book, as these book are great palate-cleansers between heavier books on my TBR list.</span>
  <a data-text-id="18259699825478986574" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_723116031" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/723116031" />
    <a title="S. Rutherford" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23553966-s-rutherford"><img alt="S. Rutherford" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1447135392p2/23553966.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/723116031?book_show_action=true">Sep 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="S. Rutherford" class="user" itemprop="url" name="S. Rutherford" href="/user/show/23553966-s-rutherford">S. Rutherford</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23553966-s-rutherford?shelf=vampire-romance">vampire-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer723116031" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer63757300562863960">Well... erm... it's not bad... I've read much worse... and the steamy parts are awesome... but the mid-beginning bothers me.<br/><br/>It starts out really good with some intense-suspense scenes, but after those scenes end, there's no weening phase or quiver. Yes, she brings the suspenseful scenes back as "knowledge" that it had happened, but there's no haunting memory, no unsureness, quivering of returning to normal life. In fact, she dumps the story right into a friendly relationship as if the character </span>
  <span id="freeText63757300562863960" style="display:none">Well... erm... it's not bad... I've read much worse... and the steamy parts are awesome... but the mid-beginning bothers me.<br /><br />It starts out really good with some intense-suspense scenes, but after those scenes end, there's no weening phase or quiver. Yes, she brings the suspenseful scenes back as "knowledge" that it had happened, but there's no haunting memory, no unsureness, quivering of returning to normal life. In fact, she dumps the story right into a friendly relationship as if the character had been friends with this other character all along.<br /><br />I'm sorry, but situations of kidnapping and terror don't just go away in the span of three or four days, especially not when that terrifying moment lasted two weeks, as she put in her book. It just doesn't work like that. It's a nightmare you never woke up from. Nightmares we suffer with in our dreams may last us all day, but a nightmare that we endured AWAKE, for two weeks mind you, will last several months, if it ever even goes away. It makes getting into her book and taking it serious very difficult.<br /><br />I found myself just skimming over and reading the dialogue to get the gist. It's all I really can do with it. I feel I've wasted my money on it.<br /><br />I'm sorry if you like this book, but it just bothers me a whole lot. Maybe it's my knowledge of the matter, and how I've done enough research to know the long-term effects of trauma.<br /><br />And on a side note, sorry if this post seemed disjointed any. I'm adding my thoughts on cop-killers and media to a blog.</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_529008199" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/529008199" />
    <a title="Brandy Dorsch" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7419211-brandy-dorsch"><img alt="Brandy Dorsch" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1509103106p2/7419211.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/529008199?book_show_action=true">Feb 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brandy Dorsch" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brandy Dorsch" href="/user/show/7419211-brandy-dorsch">Brandy Dorsch</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer529008199" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12255076347590671918">Anders has been an Enforcer for many years and has watched his fellow Enforcers fall victim to life mates one by one. When an unusual 911 call comes in that the Enforcers respond to, Anders is amazed to find he has discovered his life mate.<br/><br/>Valerie has literally just escaped from the house of Hell. She had been kidnapped and held in a cage with several other women for almost 2 weeks. She managed to stab one of her captors and call 911. When she is talking to her rescuers she doesn't know how to e</span>
  <span id="freeText12255076347590671918" style="display:none">Anders has been an Enforcer for many years and has watched his fellow Enforcers fall victim to life mates one by one. When an unusual 911 call comes in that the Enforcers respond to, Anders is amazed to find he has discovered his life mate.<br /><br />Valerie has literally just escaped from the house of Hell. She had been kidnapped and held in a cage with several other women for almost 2 weeks. She managed to stab one of her captors and call 911. When she is talking to her rescuers she doesn't know how to explain to them that she was attacked by a psycho vampire. There is no such as thing as vampires, right?<br /><br />When she is taken back to Lucien and Leigh's house for recovery she doesn't question the kindness of the ones who rescued her and finds that she is quickly falling for the sexy Enforcer, Anders. When they all realize that she is Anders life mate they attempt to show her what he really is like and a very pregnant Leigh makes a great matchmaker!<br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_528871385" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/528871385" />
    <a title="Lisarenee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2038272-lisarenee"><img alt="Lisarenee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1235941178p2/2038272.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/528871385?book_show_action=true">Feb 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lisarenee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lisarenee" href="/user/show/2038272-lisarenee">Lisarenee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2038272-lisarenee?shelf=nbrc-2013-b-reading-challenge">nbrc-2013-b-reading-challenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2038272-lisarenee?shelf=nbrc-tower-team-b-challenge-shelf">nbrc-tower-team-b-challenge-shelf</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer528871385" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5262710765359480012"><b>My Synopsis:</b><br/>Kidnapped with her life and the lives of six other woman in jeopardy, she waited for her chance. When it was finally her turn she pretended to be drugged, which she would have been, if she had eaten the food. She searched for a weapon or some means of escape as <i>he</i> dragged her through the house, and when the opportunity presented itself, she took it. She ironically staked the large man she and the other captives referred to as Igor. He wasn't her only concern, however. She knew he was</span>
  <span id="freeText5262710765359480012" style="display:none"><b>My Synopsis:</b><br />Kidnapped with her life and the lives of six other woman in jeopardy, she waited for her chance. When it was finally her turn she pretended to be drugged, which she would have been, if she had eaten the food. She searched for a weapon or some means of escape as <i>he</i> dragged her through the house, and when the opportunity presented itself, she took it. She ironically staked the large man she and the other captives referred to as Igor. He wasn't her only concern, however. She knew he was just preparing her for his <i>master's</i> sick amusement. For the man who thought himself a vampire and kept 7 woman at a time, one for each day of the week, locked in cages. As she was on the phone with 911 she heard the telltale sound of the garage door opening. She'd have to rescue herself and hope the police got there in time to save the others. Before she could go very far, however, she passed out from loss of blood from a wound inflicted on her during her fight for freedom. <br /><br />Now in the protective custody of Immortal Council's Enforcers, she'll be put to the test. For Valerie is special in more ways and than one. She's Anders' life mate. Will she be able to love the very type of man who held her hostage? Will she be able to discern the difference between the rogue immortal that attacked her and the one who, if she says yes, could be her life mate? Or will the horror that vampires really do exist be too much? And with her captor still on the loose is she truly safe? Anders will have his work cut out for him to convince Valerie he's worth it and keep her safe. <br /><br /><b>My Thoughts:</b><br />This is the eighteenth book in the Argeneau series. While most would probably consider the beings Ms. Sands has created vampires, she's added a scientific twist by letting bio-engineered nanos be the explanation behind her immortals' need for blood and their longevity. Created by the physicians of Atlantis just prior to its sinking, the scientifically advanced civilization had created the nanos. By introducing them into a person's blood stream, the nanos both repair and enhance the human body. They also need more blood than one human being alone can create, hence immortals require additional blood. I have to admit I love the whole concept of nanos as being the basis for the immortality of Lynsay Sands' vampire like beings. Since the Argeneau series began, nanos have been popping up right and left within many books. I guess I'm not the only fan.<br /><br />In Immortal Ever After, Valerie Moyer is a vet who's decided to take some time off from her practice to brush up her veterinarian skills and mend her wounded heart. Before she could even start her classes, however, she was snatched off the street and kidnapped. From a kidnapper's perspective, she was the perfect victim with no family or friends in the area to notice her disappearance. She, however, was made of sterner stuff and she fought back. I liked how even though Valerie was in a bad situation she managed to keep her head and escape. <br /><br />Anders was a fun character. I liked how he was so unsure about Valerie, and who could blame him? Just because you know someone is your life mate doesn't mean they'll actually want to be yours. There are any number of reasons or situations which could contribute to them not accepting you as a potential mate. They could be in another fully committed relationship when you find them, they could think you're a totally nut job when you try to explain what you are, or they could be totally traumatized by some rogue vampire who kidnapped and terrorized them. Lucky Anders, well, not really. Anders will need to take things nice and slow if he wants any hope of gaining her trust and love. <br /><br />Overall, I gave this one <b>4 out of 5 roses.</b> It was a nice combination of romance and suspense. I enjoyed the mystery of who the rogue was and the suspense created by not knowing if he would still prove to be a danger to Valerie. I enjoyed learning more about Anders and his background. I loved Valerie and the fact she rescued herself. I also liked how she took the news that vampires, er, immortals truly do exist. Additionally, I loved how we were able to see how some of the other characters from previous books were doing. I confess, I fell a little more in love with Lucian, whose house Valerie stays at, and his attitude that what his woman wants his woman gets. lol A very fun and enjoyable read. On the Lisarenee Romance Rating Scale, this one gets a <b>STEAM</b>--too hot for a fan, but you still have a handle on things. You should use extreme caution when reading a book with this rating in public. People may inquire as to why you looked flustered and flushed. <br /><br />If you'd like to see more of my reviews, please visit my blog at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.seducedbyabook.com">www.seducedbyabook.com</a> I'd greatly appreciate it. :)</span>
  <a data-text-id="5262710765359480012" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13118052-laura?shelf=favorite-s">favorite-s</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13118052-laura?shelf=finding-love">finding-love</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2140559585" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9808367518914555112">Immortal Ever After, explains Anders bi-racial background and the amusing love story of Anders and Valerie. They are introduced to each other during a raid on a house of rouge vampire who has kidnapped several women for his own personal needs. Their love story also revolves round Lucian and Leigh Argeneau baby pending birth. I was truly surprised and enjoyed their story, and all the other shenanigan's when the Argeneau circle is involved. </span>

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('uf6E4BrCXOGIYft+x9dRj6lNdixSOu2rDPcYXLM3FoFpNkQIwwRKZIisgI12LfvSSXThAjS/RdDdG34NeX4Yrg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('n+IO6G5JFeyFXzjj1DcMG4j0ZmXQUqfAarWTjCmyANhPKs4At48DaYWSQxBlzaZGaM3xS7bXD7u7WfXd4/sO9w==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer6915971424618975345">LYNSAY SANDS is the nationally bestselling author who is known for her hysterical historicals as well as the popular Argeneau/Rogue Hunter vampire series. With her witty and charming personality, Sands describes books as, “Waking dreams or stories, tales to amuse, entertain and distract us from everyday life.” She’s been writing stories since grade school and considers herself incredibly lucky to </span>
  <span id="freeText6915971424618975345" style="display:none">LYNSAY SANDS is the nationally bestselling author who is known for her hysterical historicals as well as the popular Argeneau/Rogue Hunter vampire series. With her witty and charming personality, Sands describes books as, “Waking dreams or stories, tales to amuse, entertain and distract us from everyday life.” She’s been writing stories since grade school and considers herself incredibly lucky to be able to make a career out of it. Her hope is that readers can get away from their everyday stress through her stories, and if there are occasional uncontrollable fits of laughter, that’s just a big bonus. Visit her official website at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.lynsaysands.net">www.lynsaysands.net</a>.<br /><br /></span>

      <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/work/quotes/21397455-immortal-ever-after">Quotes from Immortal Ever After</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;Can I see your fangs again? Valerie asked<br /><br />Er.... Justin said, then spotted Anders and smiled with relief. Anders, buddy. Show your woman your fangs.<br /><br />Shy, Bricker? You? Anders asked dryly, moving forward again as Valerie glanced around to smile at him.<br /><br />Nah. I just don't want to show you up by letting her see how much bigger my fangs are than yours, Justin responded.<br /><br />Actually, I saw Ander's fangs at his house this afternoon and they're bigger than yours, Valerie said at once and then as Anders reached her side , she glanced at him and asked, Why? Is it like big fangs, big feet, big -?&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/826487-can-i-see-your-fangs-again-valerie-asked-er-justin">12 likes</a>
            </nobr>
            <div class="clear"></div>
          </div>
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;So? When do you want to be turned?” “I didn’t agree to turn,” Valerie squawked with amazement. “You haven’t, but you will,” he said with a shrug. “What makes you think that?” she asked warily. “Because if you don’t, I’m going to have to wipe your memories and have you returned to your life and neither of us wants that,” he said simply. “Anders said I could have time to decide,” Valerie protested, and then frowned and added, “And what do you mean, neither of us wants that? Why would you care?” “You saved my wife and children, Valerie. And Leigh adores you. You’re family now.” “Oh.” She stared at him nonplussed, wondering if he meant that. “I mean it,” he said firmly. “Leigh has decided it’s so, so it’s so. She’d be disappointed if you didn’t become one of us and I won’t have her disappointed.” Valerie scowled slightly. The last part sounded like a threat. “As for Anders saying you could have time to decide,” Lucian continued. “What do you need time for? The nanos have paired you, you’re meant to be together.” “You make it sound so simple,” she said wearily. “It is simple. Don’t make it hard.” “Great, the nanos paired us. But what about love?” she asked. Lucian shifted impatiently. “Do you like him?” “Yes,” she admitted. “Respect him?” She nodded. “Trust him?” “Of course,” she said without hesitation. Lucian nodded and said dryly, “I don’t need to ask if you want him sexually.” Valerie flushed and raised her chin. “All those things combined make up love,” Lucian assured her. “Whether you realize it or not, you already do love him.” Valerie swallowed, knowing in her heart he was right. She bit her lip, and then blurted, “But does he love me?” “Ah.” Lucian nodded. “So that’s the holdup, is it? He hasn’t said it yet.” Valerie sighed and looked away, muttering, “When he asked me to be his life mate he went on about finding peace and being able to relax and be at peace. It was all peace, peace, peace,” she added with frustration and glanced to Lucian, eyes narrowing when she caught his lips twitching. If he laughed at her, she would— “Don’t you feel at peace with him?” he asked, and then added, “When you’re not hot and bothered, I mean.” “Well, yeah, but—” “But you want to hear that he loves you,” Lucian said and shrugged. “I guess you’ll have to ask him then.” “Ask him if he loves me?” she asked with dismay. Lucian sighed with exasperation. “You took on Igor and staked him, saving yourself and six other women in the process—” “Four,” she corrected unhappily. “Two died, remember.” “And then,” he continued heavily, ignoring her interruption. “You took on Ambrose and saved my wife and unborn twins by crashing the van you were all in and repeatedly bashing the man over the head until help got there. You are not a coward, Valerie, so stop acting like one. Ask him. And when he says yes he loves you, I will personally oversee the turning and pay for the wedding.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/8939325-so-when-do-you-want-to-be-turned-i-didn-t">2 likes</a>
            </nobr>
            <div class="clear"></div>
          </div>
